class="theme-doc-sidebar-item-link theme-doc-sidebar-item-link-level-2 menu__list-item"><a class="menu__link" tabindex="0" href="/weaviate/tutorials/tokenization"><span title="Configure tokenization for keyword search" class="linkLabel_WmDU">Configure tokenization for keyword search</span></a></li><li class="theme-doc-sidebar-item-link theme-doc-sidebar-item-link-level-2 menu__list-item"><a .2-.062.399-.172.547l-4.996 7.492a.982.982 0 01-.828.454H1c-.55 0-1-.453-1-1 0-.2.059-.403.168-.551l4.629-6.942L.168 3.078A.939.939 0 010 2.528c0-.548.45-.997 1-.997h2.996c.352 0 .649.18.828.45L9.82 0"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></aside><main class="docMainContainer_TBSr"><div class="container padding-top--md padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_z5aJ"><div class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/tutorials"><span>Tutorials</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Quick tour of Weaviate</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Quick tour of Weaviate</h1></header><p>This tutorial will show you how to use Weaviate Cloud to:</p>
<ol>
<li class=""><strong>Set up a Weaviate instance.</strong></li>
<li class=""><strong>Import and vectorize your data.</strong></li>
<li class=""><strong>Perform a semantic search and retrieval augmented generation (RAG).</strong></li>
</ol>
<!-- -->
<hr>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="prerequisites">Prerequisites<a href="#prerequisites" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Prerequisites" title="Direct link to Prerequisites" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>In order to perform Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) in the last step, you will need a <a href="https://dashboard.cohere.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Cohere</a> account. You can use a free Cohere trial API key.</p>
<p>If you have another preferred <a class="" href="/weaviate/model-providers">model provider</a>, you can use that instead of Cohere.</p>
<hr>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-1-set-up-weaviate">Step 1: Set up Weaviate<a href="#step-1-set-up-weaviate" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 1: Set up Weaviate" title="Direct link to Step 1: Set up Weaviate" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="11-install-a-client-library">1.1 Install a client library<a href="#11-install-a-client-library" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 1.1 Install a client library" title="Direct link to 1.1 Install a client library" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>We recommend using a <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries">client library</a> to work with Weaviate. Follow the instructions below to install one of the official client libraries, available in <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/python">Python</a>, <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/typescript">JavaScript/TypeScript</a>, <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/go">Go</a>, and <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/java">Java</a>.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="java">Java v5 (Deprecated)</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="12-connect-to-weaviate-cloud">1.2 Connect to Weaviate Cloud<a href="#12-connect-to-weaviate-cloud" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 1.2 Connect to Weaviate Cloud" title="Direct link to 1.2 Connect to Weaviate Cloud" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>How to create a Weaviate Cloud Sandbox</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>Go to the <a href="https://console.weaviate.cloud" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Weaviate Cloud console</a> and create a free Sandbox instance.</p><div style="position:relative;padding-bottom:calc(54.10879629629629% + 50px);height:0"><iframe id="mk6l470aqk" src="https://app.guideflow.com/embed/mk6l470aqk" width="100%" height="100%" style="overflow:hidden;position:absolute;border:none" scrolling="no" allow="clipboard-read; clipboard-write" allowfullscreen="" allowtransparency="true"></iframe><script src="https://app.guideflow.com/assets/opt.js" data-iframe-id="mk6l470aqk"></script></div><br><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><ul>
<li class="">Cluster provisioning typically takes 1-3 minutes.</li>
<li class="">When the cluster is ready, Weaviate Cloud displays a checkmark (<code>✔️</code>) next to the cluster name.</li>
<li class="">Note that Weaviate Cloud adds a random suffix to sandbox cluster names to ensure uniqueness.</li>
</ul></div></div><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>TIP: Use the latest Weaviate version!</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>When possible, try to use the latest Weaviate version.
New releases include cutting-edge features, performance enhancements, and critical security updates to keep your application safe and up-to-date.</p></div></div></div></div></details>
<p>Now you can connect to your Weaviate instance. You will need the:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>REST Endpoint URL</strong> and the</li>
<li class=""><strong>Administrator API Key</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<p>You can retrieve them both from the <a href="https://console.weaviate.cloud" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">WCD console</a> as shown in the interactive example below.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>New clusters with Weaviate version <code>v1.30</code> (or later) have <a class="" href="/weaviate/configuration/rbac">RBAC (Role-Based Access Control)</a> enabled by default. These clusters don&#x27;t come with API keys, you will need to create an API key yourself and assign it a role (<code>admin</code>, <code>viewer</code> or a custom role).</p></div></div>
<div style="position:relative;padding-bottom:calc(54.10879629629629% + 50px);height:0"><iframe id="ok8l954sxr" src="https://app.guideflow.com/embed/ok8l954sxr" width="100%" height="100%" style="overflow:hidden;position:absolute;border:none" scrolling="no" allow="clipboard-read; clipboard-write" allowfullscreen="" allowtransparency="true"></iframe><script src="https://app.guideflow.com/assets/opt.js" data-iframe-id="ok8l954sxr"></script></div>
<br>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>REST vs gRPC endpoints</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Weaviate supports both REST and gRPC protocols. For Weaviate Cloud deployments, you only need to provide the REST endpoint URL - the client will automatically configure gRPC.</p></div></div>
<p>Once you have the <strong>REST Endpoint URL</strong> and the <strong>admin API key</strong>, you can connect to the Sandbox instance, and work with Weaviate.</p>
<p>The example below shows how to connect to Weaviate and perform a basic operation, like checking the cluster status.</p>

<p>If you did not see any errors, you are ready to proceed. We will replace the simple cluster status check with more meaningful operations in the next steps.</p>
<hr>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-2-populate-the-database">Step 2: Populate the database<a href="#step-2-populate-the-database" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 2: Populate the database" title="Direct link to Step 2: Populate the database" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Now, we can populate our database by first defining a collection and then adding data.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="21-define-a-collection">2.1 Define a collection<a href="#21-define-a-collection" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 2.1 Define a collection" title="Direct link to 2.1 Define a collection" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>What is a collection?</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>A collection is a set of objects that share the same data structure, like a table in relational databases or a collection in NoSQL databases. A collection also includes additional configurations that define how the data objects are stored and indexed.</p></div></div>
<p>The following example creates a <em>collection</em> called <code>Question</code> with:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <a class="" href="/weaviate/model-providers/weaviate/embeddings">Weaviate Embeddings</a> service for creating vectors during ingestion &amp; queries.</li>
</ul>

aria-hidden="true"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><p>The collection also contains a configuration for the generative (RAG) integration:</p><ul>
<li class="">OpenAI <a class="" href="/weaviate/model-providers/openai/generative">generative AI integrations</a> for retrieval augmented generation (RAG).</li>
</ul><div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># Best practice: store your credentials in environment variables</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># export WEAVIATE_URL=&quot;YOUR_INSTANCE_URL&quot;  # Your Weaviate instance URL</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># export WEAVIATE_API_KEY=&quot;YOUR_API_KEY&quot;   # Your Weaviate instance API key</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">curl -X POST \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">-H &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">-H &quot;Authorization: Bearer $WEAVIATE_API_KEY&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">-d &#x27;{</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  &quot;class&quot;: &quot;Question&quot;,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  &quot;vectorizer&quot;: &quot;text2vec-weaviate&quot;,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  &quot;moduleConfig&quot;: {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    &quot;text2vec-weaviate&quot;: {},</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    &quot;generative-cohere&quot;: {}</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">}&#x27; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">&quot;$WEAVIATE_URL/v1/schema&quot;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div></div>
<p>Run this code to create the collection to which you can add data.</p>
<!-- -->
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Do you prefer a different setup?</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>If you prefer a different model provider integration, or prefer to import your own vectors, see one of the following guides:</p>
<!-- -->
<!-- -->
<div class="cardsSection_Ezca smallCards_eRph"><a class="card_OoQD" href="/weaviate/model-providers"><div class="cardHeader_rXdg"><i class="fas fa-puzzle-piece cardIcon_K4xK"></i><span class="cardTitle_TsZq">Prefer a different model provider?</span></div><p class="cardDescription__QXy">See the embedding model providers page for information on other available vectorizers, such as AWS, Cohere, Google, and many more.</p></a><a class="card_OoQD" href="/weaviate/starter-guides/custom-vectors"><div class="cardHeader_rXdg"><i class="fas fa-project-diagram cardIcon_K4xK"></i><span class="cardTitle_TsZq">You have precomputed embeddings?</span></div><p class="cardDescription__QXy">If you prefer to add custom vectors yourself along with the object data, see the Bring Your Own Vectors starter guide.</p></a></div></div></div></details>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="22-add-objects">2.2 Add objects<a href="#22-add-objects" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 2.2 Add objects" title="Direct link to 2.2 Add objects" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>We can now add data to our collection.</p>
<p>The following example:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Loads objects, and</li>
<li class="">Adds objects to the target collection (<code>Question</code>) using a batch process.</li>
</ul>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>Batch imports</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>(<a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-objects/import">Batch imports</a>) are the most efficient way to add large amounts of data, as it sends multiple objects in a single request. See the <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-objects/import">How-to: Batch import</a> guide for more information.</p></div></div>

style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Free up resources</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2"></div></div><p>During a batch import, any failed objects can be obtained through <code>batch.failed_objects</code>. Additionally, a running count of failed objects is maintained and can be accessed through <code>batch.number_errors</code> within the context manager. This counter can be used to stop the import process in order to investigate the failed objects or references. Find out more about error handling on the Python client <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/python/notes-best-practices#error-handling">reference page</a>.</p></div></div><div <li class="">Download the <code>jeopardy_tiny.json</code> file from <a href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/weaviate-tutorials/quickstart/main/data/jeopardy_tiny.json" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">here</a> before running the following script.</li>
<li class="">This assumes you have <code>jq</code> installed.</li>
</ul></div></div><div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># Best practice: store your credentials in environment variables</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># export WEAVIATE_URL=&quot;YOUR_INSTANCE_URL&quot;  # Your Weaviate instance URL</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># export WEAVIATE_API_KEY=&quot;YOUR_API_KEY&quot;   # Your Weaviate instance API key</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># Set batch size</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">BATCH_ENDPOINT=&quot;$WEAVIATE_URL/v1/batch/objects&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">BATCH_SIZE=100</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># Read the JSON file and loop through its entries</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">lines_processed=0</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">batch_data=&quot;{\&quot;objects\&quot;: [&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">cat jeopardy_tiny.json | jq -c &#x27;.[]&#x27; | while read line; do</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  # Concatenate lines</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  line=$(echo &quot;$line&quot; | jq &quot;{class: \&quot;Question\&quot;, properties: {answer: .Answer, question: .Question, category: .Category}}&quot;)</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  if [ $lines_processed -eq 0 ]; then</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    batch_data+=$line</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  else</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    batch_data+=&quot;,$line&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  fi</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  lines_processed=$((lines_processed + 1))</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  # If the batch is full, send it to the API using curl</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  if [ $lines_processed -eq $BATCH_SIZE ]; then</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    batch_data+=&quot;]}&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    curl -X POST &quot;$BATCH_ENDPOINT&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">         -H &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">         -H &quot;Authorization: Bearer $WEAVIATE_API_KEY&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">         -d &quot;$batch_data&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    echo &quot;&quot; # Print a newline for better output formatting</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    # Reset the batch data and counter</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    lines_processed=0</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    batch_data=&quot;{\&quot;objects\&quot;: [&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  fi</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">done</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># Send the remaining data (if any) to the API using curl</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">if [ $lines_processed -ne 0 ]; then</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  batch_data+=&quot;]}&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  curl -X POST &quot;$BATCH_ENDPOINT&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">       -H &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">       -H &quot;Authorization: Bearer $WEAVIATE_API_KEY&quot; \</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">       -d &quot;$batch_data&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  echo &quot;&quot; # Print a newline for better output formatting</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">fi</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div></div>
<p>Run this code to add the demo data.</p>
<hr>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-3-queries">Step 3: Queries<a href="#step-3-queries" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 3: Queries" title="Direct link to Step 3: Queries" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Weaviate provides a wide range of query tools to help you find the right data. We will try a few searches here.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="semantic-search">3.1 Semantic search<a href="#semantic-search" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 3.1 Semantic search" title="Direct link to 3.1 Semantic search" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Semantic search finds results based on meaning. This is called <code>nearText</code> in Weaviate.</p>
<p>The following example searches for 2 objects whose meaning is most similar to that of <code>biology</code>.</p>

<p>Run this code to perform the query. Our query found entries for <code>DNA</code> and <code>species</code>.</p>

<p>If you inspect the full response, you will see that the word <code>biology</code> does not appear anywhere.</p>
<p>Even so, Weaviate was able to return biology-related entries. This is made possible by <em>vector embeddings</em> that capture meaning. Under the hood, semantic search is powered by vectors, or vector embeddings.</p>
<p>Here is a diagram showing the workflow in Weaviate.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Where did the vectors come from?</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Weaviate used the <strong>Weaviate Embeddings</strong> service to generate a vector embedding for each object during import. During the query, Weaviate similarly converted the query (<code>biology</code>) into a vector.</p><p>As we mentioned above, this is optional. See <a class="" href="/weaviate/starter-guides/custom-vectors">Starter Guide: Bring Your Own Vectors</a> if you would prefer to provide your own vectors.</p></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>More search types available</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Weaviate is capable of many types of searches. See, for example, our how-to guides on <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/similarity">similarity searches</a>, <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/bm25">keyword searches</a>, <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/hybrid">hybrid searches</a>, and <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/filters">filtered searches</a>.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="32-retrieval-augmented-generation">3.2 Retrieval augmented generation<a href="#32-retrieval-augmented-generation" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to 3.2 Retrieval augmented generation" title="Direct link to 3.2 Retrieval augmented generation" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Retrieval augmented generation (RAG), also called generative search, combines the power of generative AI models such as large language models (LLMs) with the up-to-date truthfulness of a database.</p>
<p>RAG works by prompting a large language model (LLM) with a combination of a <em>user query</em> and <em>data retrieved from a database</em>.</p>
<p>This diagram shows the RAG workflow in Weaviate.</p>
<!-- -->
<p>The following example combines the same search (for <code>biology</code>) with a prompt to generate a tweet.</p>
<!-- -->

style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-csharp codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># Best practice: store your credentials in URL</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># export WEAVIATE_API_KEY=&quot;YOUR_API_KEY&quot;     # Your Weaviate instance API key</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"># export COHERE_APIKEY=&quot;YOUR_API_KEY&quot;   # Your Cohere API key</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">echo class="token plain">    Get {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      Question (</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        limit: 2</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        nearText: {</span><br></span><span {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              task: \&quot;\&quot;\&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">                Write a tweet with emojis about these facts.</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              \&quot;\&quot;\&quot;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" $WEAVIATE_URL/v1/graphql</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Cohere API key in the header</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Note that this code includes an additional header for the Cohere API key. Weaviate uses this key to access the Cohere generative AI model and perform retrieval augmented generation (RAG).</p></div></div>
<p>Run this code to perform the query. Here is one possible response (your response will likely be different).</p>
<div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">🧬 In 1953 Watson &amp; Crick built a model of the molecular structure of DNA, the gene-carrying substance! 🧬🔬</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">🦢 2000 news: the Gunnison sage grouse isn&#x27;t just another northern sage grouse, but a new species! 🦢🌿 #ScienceFacts #DNA #SpeciesClassification</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The response should be new, yet familiar. This is because you have seen the entries above for <code>DNA</code> and <code>species</code> in the <a href="#semantic-search" class="">semantic search</a> section.</p>
<p>The power of RAG comes from the ability to transform your own data. Weaviate helps you in this journey by making it easy to perform a combined search &amp; generation in just a few lines of code.</p>
<hr>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="recap">Recap<a href="#recap" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Recap" title="Direct link to Recap" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>In this quickstart guide, you:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Created a Serverless Weaviate sandbox instance on Weaviate Cloud.</li>
<li class="">Defined a collection and added data.</li>
<li class="">Performed queries, including:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class="">Semantic search, and</li>
<li class="">Retrieval augmented generation.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Where to go next is up to you. We include some suggested steps and resources below.</p>
<hr>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="questions-and-feedback">Questions and feedback<a href="#questions-and-feedback" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Questions and feedback" title="Direct link to Questions and feedback" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<p>If you have any questions or feedback, let us know in the <a href="https://forum.weaviate.io/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">user forum</a>.</p>
